3019363 = {
	name="Ролланд"	# a lord
	dynasty=363

	religion="the_seven"
	culture="sisterman"

	father=3017363
	mother=4017363

	8187.1.1 = {add_trait=skilled_warrior}
	8195.3.7 = { #Blackfyre Rebellion
		effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { start_date = 8196.6.1 } }
				set_defacto_liege = ROOT
				set_character_flag = against_king
				set_character_flag = against_loyal_liege
				any_demesne_title = {
					limit = { 
						OR = {
							tier = COUNT
							tier = DUKE
						}
					}				
					set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 4 } #vale
				}
				e_iron_throne = {
					holder_scope = { 
						opinion = {
							modifier = opinion_joined_rebellion
							who = ROOT
							years = 20
						}
					}
				}
				k_daemon_blackfyres_host = {
					holder_scope = { 
						opinion = {
							who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_joined_cause
						}
						reverse_opinion = {
							modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader
							who = ROOT
							years = 100
						}
						ROOT = {
							join_attacker_wars = PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	8212.1.1 = {
		death = {
			death_reason = death_execution
			killer = 77026 #executed at whitewalls by bloodraven
		}	
	}
}

				limit = { is_ruler = no }

						ROOT = { move_character = PREV }
					}
				}
			}	
		}
	}

		remove_trait=kingsguard
		add_trait=nightswatch
		effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_ruler = no }

					holder_scope = {
						ROOT = { move_character = PREV }
					}
				}
			}	
		}
